019862,003487:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019863,003488: 
019864,003489:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
019865,003490:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
019866,003491:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
019867,003492:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
019868,003493: 
019869,003494:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019870,003495:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1) BY ENDIDLE
019871,003496:                                                                                                  #                2) BY NVSUBUSY
019872,003497:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
019873,003498:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019874,003499:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
019875,003500:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
019876,003501: 
019877,003502:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
019878,003503:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
019879,003504:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
019880,003505:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
019881,003506:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
019882,003507: 
019883,003508:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
019884,003509:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019885,003510:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
019886,003511:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019887,003512:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019888,003513: 
019889,003514:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
019890,003515:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
019891,003516:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
019892,003517: 
019893,003518: 
019894,003519:                                                                                                  #  .
019895,003520: 
019896,003521:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
019897,003522:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
019898,003523:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
019899,003524:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019900,003525: 
019901,003526:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019902,003527:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
019903,003528:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
019904,003529:                                                                                                  #  1)    DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
019905,003530:                                                                                                  #        IS EXCEEDED.
019906,003531:                                                                                                  #  2)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 464 

019908,003533:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019909,003534: 
019910,003535:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
019911,003536:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
019912,003537:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
019913,003538:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
019914,003539:    4443           10647                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
019915,003540:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
019916,003541: 
019917,003542:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
019918,003543:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
019919,003544: 
019920,003545: 04,2647                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
019921,003546: 04,2647                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019922,003547: 04,2647           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
019923,003548: 04,2650           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019924,003549: 04,2651           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
019925,003550: 04,2652           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
019926,003551: 04,2653           30001                           CA       L                                     
019927,003552: 04,2654           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
019928,003553: 04,2655           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019929,003554: 
019930,003555:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
019931,003556:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
019932,003557:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
019933,003558:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
019934,003559:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
019935,003560: 
019936,003561:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
019937,003562:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019938,003563:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019939,003564:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
019940,003565:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019941,003566:    4450           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019942,003567:    4451           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
019943,003568:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019944,003569:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
019945,003570:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
019946,003571:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
019947,003572:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
019948,003573:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
019949,003574: 
019950,003575:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
019951,003576:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
019952,003577:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
019953,003578: 
019954,003579:    4457           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT
019955,003580:    4460           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST
019956,003581:    4461           44736                           CS       BIT14

Page 465 

019958,003583:    4462           00004                           INHINT                                         
019959,003584:    4463           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              
019960,003585:    4464           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019961,003586:    4465           11043                           CCS      DSPLIST                               
019962,003587:    4466           04470                           TC       +2                                    
019963,003588:    4467           04473                           TC       RELDSP2                               #  LIST EMPTY
019964,003589:    4470           34755                           CAF      ZERO                                  
019965,003590:    4471           57043                           XCH      DSPLIST                               
019966,003591:    4472           05137                           TC       JOBWAKE                               
019967,003592:    4473           00003        RELDSP2            RELINT                                         
019968,003593:    4474           44747                           CS       BIT5                                  #  TURN OFF KEY RELEASE LIGHT
019969,003594:    4475           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11)

020098,003723:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF:
020099,003724:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
020100,003725:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
020101,003726:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
020102,003727:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROS THE 'TEST ALARM' OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
020103,003728:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS 'CAUTION RESET' TO 1.
020104,003729:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
020105,003730: 
020106,003731: 40,3603                                           SETLOC   DOPROC     +2                         
020107,003732: 40,3603                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN

020109,003734: 40,3604           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #  LIGHT RESET LEAVES DSPLOCK UNCHANGED.
020110,003735: 40,3605           00004                           INHINT

020112,003737: 40,3607           00006                           EXTEND

020115,003740: 40,3612           71036                           MASK     DSPTAB     +11D                       #  TURNING OFF AUTO, HOLD, FREE,
020116,003741: 40,3613           64735                           AD       BIT15                                 #  PROG ALARM, AND TRACKER.

020120,003745: 40,3617           65026                           AD       PRIO16                                #  EXISTS, THE ALARM WILL COME BACK.
